posted:Posted July 1, 2021
msg:Sure enough, a hotel with a high rating is not necessarily good, but a hotel with a low rating is definitely not good!
I came to Chengdu to live at Fairmont or Hilton before, but this time I stayed for three days. I wanted to be more convenient and stayed at Chunxi Mercure. Sure enough, there is no reason to like Accor. Although Mercure is expensive, it has surpassed many other five-star/luxury hotels in terms of environment, hygiene, service and facilities, except for the small rooms.
Because the flight was cancelled and stranded, I saw more than 300 five-star hotels and thought I had picked up a leak. As a result, I went to see-
First of all, the environment of the location is general, and there is no business circle around. It is said that it is close to the scenic spots, but it is not close.
Secondly, I feel that the facilities are slightly old, which may be the reason for the decoration style. As a hotel with more than 20 floors and hundreds of rooms, can you believe that there are only 3 elevators? ! It takes a long time to wait for the elevator every time, and the elevator doesn't feel as fast as taking the stairs... I must also mention the network, because the signal is poor and I changed the room (explaining that it is upgrading), the result is still poor...
Once again the sanitary conditions, the carpet is very dirty, the sink is not cleaned, and there is still something on the bath towel... I dare not take a closer look at the others...
Service again, from the front desk to the room, the service can not be said to be poor, but it gives a great sense of distance, it feels very indifferent and not enthusiastic, I think it is unqualified as a luxury hotel.
Some hotels and even homestays, although the rooms are small and low-priced and limited by hardware facilities, do not have many services, but they are trying to be a good part of the people, clean and tidy services are warm and thoughtful, and many details are eye-catching. But this time, the overall feeling is that in the post-epidemic era, the hotel industry is picking up and intensifying, and this is the level of a small county hotel or a 5-10-year-old economical hotel in a big city.
